# Fix Form Field Rendering for Custom Widget Attributes

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/django--674eda1c (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/django--674eda1c (mirror of django/django)
**Your Role:** Junior Developer — Forms Team
**Access Scope:** You have **write access** to `django/forms/` only. You may **read** `django/core/`, `django/utils/`, and `django/db/models/fields/` to understand patterns and dependencies. You must NOT modify any files outside `django/forms/`.

## Context

You are a junior developer on the Forms team. Your team owns the `django/forms/` package. Other packages are maintained by other teams — you can read their code to understand how things work, but you must not modify their files.

## Bug Report

**Reported by:** Frontend Integration Team
**Severity:** High
**Ticket:** FORMS-2847

When a form field widget specifies custom HTML attributes through a `build_attrs` call, certain attribute values are not properly escaped when they contain special characters like quotes or ampersands. This causes malformed HTML in rendered forms.

The issue specifically affects how widget attributes are merged and rendered. The expected behavior is that all attribute values should be properly escaped for HTML output, but somewhere in the attribute building and rendering pipeline, raw values are being passed through without escaping.

### Reproduction

A form field with a widget configured to include an attribute like `data-label='Value with "quotes"'` renders the quotes unescaped in the final HTML, breaking the DOM structure.

**YOU MUST IMPLEMENT CODE CHANGES.**

### Requirements

1. Fix the attribute escaping issue in Django's forms widget rendering pipeline
2. Ensure all widget attribute values are properly HTML-escaped before rendering
3. The fix should handle edge cases: quotes, ampersands, angle brackets, and None values
4. Must not break existing widget rendering behavior for normal attribute values
5. Valid Python syntax
6. **All changes must be within `django/forms/` only** — you do not have write access to other packages

## Success Criteria

- Widget attributes with special characters are properly HTML-escaped
- Fix is within `django/forms/` package only
- Existing widget rendering continues to work
- Valid Python syntax

196-usertool_resultBash
def conditional_escape(text):
    """
    Similar to escape(), except that it doesn't operate on pre-escaped strings.

    This function relies on the __html__ convention used both by Django's
    SafeData class and by third-party libraries like markupsafe.
    """
    if isinstance(text, Promise):
        text = str(text)
    if hasattr(text, "__html__"):
        return text.__html__()

219-assistanttool_useBash
220-usertool_resultBash
# Widget Attribute Escaping Fix

## Problem
Widget attributes containing special characters (quotes, ampersands, angle brackets) were not being properly HTML-escaped when rendered, potentially causing malformed HTML or security issues.

## Root Cause
The Django template filter `stringformat` is marked with `is_safe=True`, which prevents Django's auto-escaping system from escaping the output. In the widget rendering templates, `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` was being used to render attribute values and input values, which resulted in unescaped HTML special characters appearing in the output.

## Solution
Replaced all occurrences of `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` with `{{ value|escape }}` in the following template files:

1. django/forms/templates/django/forms/attrs.html
2. django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/attrs.html
3. django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/input.html
4. django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/select_option.html

The `escape` filter uses `conditional_escape()` which:
- Properly escapes HTML special characters: &, ", ', <, >
- Does NOT double-escape values already marked as safe (SafeString)
- Converts values to strings before escaping (like stringformat did)

## Impact
- Widget attributes with special characters are now properly escaped
- Existing functionality is preserved (SafeString values still work)
- All form widgets that include these templates will benefit from the fix

230-assistanttext-
Excellent! I've successfully fixed the form field widget attribute escaping issue. Here's a summary of the changes:

## Summary of Changes

**Issue**: Form widget attributes with special characters (quotes, ampersands, angle brackets) were not being properly HTML-escaped when rendered, causing malformed HTML.

**Root Cause**: The Django template filter `stringformat` is marked with `is_safe=True`, which prevents Django's auto-escaping system from escaping values. This meant attribute values were being passed through without proper HTML escaping.

**Solution**: I replaced `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` with `{{ value|escape }}` in 4 template files within `django/forms/`:

1. **django/forms/templates/django/forms/attrs.html** - Used for generic form attributes
2. **django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/attrs.html** - Used for widget-specific attributes
3. **django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/input.html** - Used for input widget values
4. **django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/select_option.html** - Used for option widget values

**How the Fix Works**:
- The `escape` filter uses Django's `conditional_escape()` function
- It properly escapes HTML special characters: `&` → `&amp;`, `"` → `&quot;`, `'` → `&#x27;`, `<` → `&lt;`, `>` → `&gt;`
- It does NOT double-escape values already marked as safe (SafeString)
- It converts values to strings before escaping (maintaining the behavior of `stringformat`)

**Impact**:
- Widget attributes with special characters are now properly HTML-escaped
- All form widgets that render these templates benefit from the fix
- Existing functionality is preserved; SafeString attributes still work correctly
- No breaking changes to existing widget rendering

All changes are contained within the `django/forms/` package as requir

#!/usr/bin/env python
"""
Test script to verify widget attribute escaping works correctly.
"""
import os
import sys
import django

# Add the workspace to the path
sys.path.insert(0, '/workspace')

# Configure Django settings
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'tests.settings')

# Setup Django
from django.conf import settings
if not settings.configured:
    settings.configure(
        DEBUG=True,
        DATABASES={'default': {'ENGINE': 'django.db.backends.sqlite3'}},
        INSTALLED_APPS=['django.contrib.contenttypes', 'django.contrib.auth'],
        SECRET_KEY='test-secret-key',
        TEMPLATES=[{
            'BACKEND': 'django.template.backends.django.DjangoTemplates',
            'DIRS': [],
            'APP_DIRS': True,
            'OPTIONS': {
                'context_processors': [
                    'django.template.context_processors.debug',
                ],
            },
        }],
    )

django.setup()

# Now test the widget rendering
from django.forms.widgets import TextInput

def test_attribute_escaping():
    """Test that widget attributes are properly HTML-escaped."""

    # Test 1: Quotes in attribute values
    widget = TextInput(attrs={'data-label': 'Value with "quotes"'})
    html = widget.render('test', None)

    # Check if quotes are properly escaped
    assert '&quot;' in html, f"Quotes not escaped in: {html}"
    assert 'Value with "quotes"' not in html, f"Unescaped quotes found in: {html}"
    print("✓ Test 1 passed: Quotes are properly escaped")

    # Test 2: Ampersands in attribute values
    widget = TextInput(attrs={'data-text': 'foo & bar'})
    html = widget.render('test', None)

    assert '&amp;' in html, f"Ampersand not escaped in: {html}"
    assert 'foo & bar' not in html, f"Unescaped ampersand found in: {html}"

28. $ cat > /tmp/fix_summary.txt << 'EOF'
# Widget Attribute Escaping Fix

## Problem
Widget attributes containing special characters (quotes, ampersands, angle brackets) were not being properly HTML-escaped when rendered, potentially causing malformed HTML or security issues.

## Root Cause
The Django template filter `stringformat` is marked with `is_safe=True`, which prevents Django's auto-escaping system from escaping the output. In the widget rendering templates, `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` was being used to render attribute values and input values, which resulted in unescaped HTML special characters appearing in the output.

## Solution
Replaced all occurrences of `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}` with `{{ value|escape }}` in the following template files:

1. django/forms/templates/django/forms/attrs.html
2. django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/attrs.html
3. django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/input.html
4. django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/select_option.html

The `escape` filter uses `conditional_escape()` which:
- Properly escapes HTML special characters: &, ", ', <, >
- Does NOT double-escape values already marked as safe (SafeString)
- Converts values to strings before escaping (like stringformat did)

## Impact
- Widget attributes with special characters are now properly escaped
- Existing functionality is preserved (SafeString values still work)
- All form widgets that include these templates will benefit from the fix
EOF
cat /tmp/fix_summary.txt
